\FormulaThmDelta[Eindeutige Existenz eines Werts in jeder Stufe]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}
  \vdash \exists! a\in M\,\bigl((n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep a\dsep b\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\exists a\in M\,\bigl((n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \exists a\in M\,\bigl((n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)}{1,2,3}}
  \proofstep{5}{a\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{b\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{7}{(n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{8}{(n,b)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,5,6,7,8}{a=b}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep a\in M\dsep b\in M\dsep (n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\dsep (n,b)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\vdash a=b}{1,2,3,5,6,7,8}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\exists! a\in M\,\bigl((n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)}{%
    \UEI{4,5,6,7,8,9}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsubsection{Der Rekursionskern als Funktion}

\FormulaThmDelta[Der Rekursionskern ist eine Abbildung]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep x\dsep y\dsep z\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Funktionale Eindeutigkeit]{%
    m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep
    (x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\dsep (x,z)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\vdash y=z
  }{%
    m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep
    (x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\dsep (x,z)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\vdash y=z
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{(x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{(x,z)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\RecCore{m_0}{f}\subseteq \mathbb{N}\times M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}\subseteq \mathbb{N}\times M}{1,2}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{(x,y)\in \mathbb{N}\times M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B\dsep x\in A\vdash x\in B}{5,3}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4]{(x,z)\in \mathbb{N}\times M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B\dsep x\in A\vdash x\in B}{5,4}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{x\in\mathbb{N}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{(a,b)\in A\times B\vdash a\in A}{6}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{y\in M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{(a,b)\in A\times B\vdash b\in B}{6}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4]{z\in M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{(a,b)\in A\times B\vdash b\in B}{7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{y=z}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep a\in M\dsep b\in M\dsep (n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\dsep (n,b)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\vdash a=b}{1,2,8,9,10,3,4}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Totalität]{%
    m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep x\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
    \exists y\,\bigl((x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)
  }{%
    m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep x\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
    \exists y\,\bigl((x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{x\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
      \exists a\in M\,\bigl((x,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)
    }{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \exists a\in M\,\bigl((n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)}{1,2,3}}

    \proofstepwidestar[5]{a\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{(x,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,5,6]{%
      \exists y\,\bigl((x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)
    }{%
      \rEI{6}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{%
      \exists y\,\bigl((x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)
    }{%
      \rEE{4,5,6,7}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
      \makecell[l]{%
        \FormulaRefAuto{Funktion}(%
        \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}\subseteq \mathbb{N}\times M}{1,2},%
        \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep (x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\dsep (x,z)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\vdash y=z}{1,2},%
        \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep x\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \exists y\,\bigl((x,y)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\bigr)}{1,2}%
        \\ )%
      }%
    }
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\paragraph{Rekursionsgleichungen des Rekursionskerns}

\FormulaThmDelta[Anfangswert des Rekursionskerns]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{(\varnothing,m_0)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash (\varnothing,m_0)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep (x,y)\in F\vdash F(x)=y}{3,4}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Rekursionsgleichung des Rekursionskerns]{%
  \begin{aligned}
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\\
    &\vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{(n,\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\vdash (x,F(x))\in F}{4,3}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n)\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{4,3}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{(\Succ(n),f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n)))\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep a\in M\dsep (n,a)\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}\vdash (\Succ(n),f(a))\in \RecCore{m_0}{f}}{1,2,3,6,5}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{(x,y)\in F\vdash F(x)=y}{4,7}}
\end{tabproof}

\paragraph{Eindeutigkeit rekursiv definierter Abbildungen}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Eindeutigkeit rekursiv definierter Abbildungen]{%
  \begin{aligned}
    &G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep
    G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep{}\\
    &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))
    \vdash G=H
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep
  G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep
  \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep
  \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))
  \vdash G=H
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep x\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f\dsep G\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Induktionsanfang]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep{}\\
      &G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))
      \vdash G(\varnothing)=H(\varnothing)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep
    G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))
    \vdash G(\varnothing)=H(\varnothing)
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{G(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{H(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[3,4]{G(\varnothing)=H(\varnothing)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, c = b \vdash a = c}{3,4}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Induktionsschritt]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep{}\\
      &G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))\dsep{}\\
      &x\in\mathbb{N}\dsep G(x)=H(x)\vdash G(\Succ(x))=H(\Succ(x))
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep
    G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))\dsep
    x\in\mathbb{N}\dsep G(x)=H(x)\vdash G(\Succ(x))=H(\Succ(x))
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{G(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{H(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{x\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[8]{G(x)=H(x)}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,7]{G(x)\in M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{1,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[2,7]{H(x)\in M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{2,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[5]{x\in\mathbb{N}\rightarrow G(\Succ(x))=f(G(x))}{\rUE{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[5,7]{G(\Succ(x))=f(G(x))}{\rRE{11,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[6]{x\in\mathbb{N}\rightarrow H(\Succ(x))=f(H(x))}{\rUE{6}}
    \proofstepwidestar[6,7]{H(\Succ(x))=f(H(x))}{\rRE{13,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,7,8]{f(G(x))=f(H(x))}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\dsep y\in A\dsep x=y\vdash F(x)=F(y)}{9,10,8}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,6,7,8]{H(\Succ(x))=f(G(x))}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, c = b \vdash a = c}{14,15}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,6,7,8]{f(G(x))=H(\Succ(x))}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{16}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,5,6,7,8]{G(\Succ(x))=H(\Succ(x))}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a = b,\, c = b \vdash a = c}{12,17}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{G(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{H(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[7]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6,7]{G(n)=H(n)}{%
      \makecell[l]{%
        \FormulaRefAuto{P(\varnothing)\dsep [x\in\mathbb{N},P(x)]\vdots P(\Succ(x))\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash P(n)}(%
        \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{%
          G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep
          G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep
          \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep
          \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))
          \vdash G(\varnothing)=H(\varnothing)
        }{1,2,3,4,5,6},%
        \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{%
          G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep
          G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep
          \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep
          \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))\dsep
          x\in\mathbb{N}\dsep G(x)=H(x)\vdash G(\Succ(x))=H(\Succ(x))
        }{1,2,3,4,5,6},%
        \\ \quad 7%
        \\ )%
      }%
    }

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6]{\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(G(n)=H(n)\bigr)}{%
      \rUI{\rRI{7,8}}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6]{G=H}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{\forall x\in A (F(x)=G(x)) \eqvdash F=G}{9}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\subsubsection{Der Dedekindsche Rekursionssatz}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Existenz einer rekursiv definierten Abbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\\
    \vdash{}&\exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl(
      G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\qquad\qquad\qquad\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,
      G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))
    \Bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\vdash \exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl(G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\Bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f\dsep G}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{5}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2,5}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))={}\\
      &f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))}{1,2,5}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))={}\\
      &\qquad f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \rUI{\rRI{5,6}}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\RecCore{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))={}\\
      &\qquad f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rAI{4,7}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl({}\\
      &\qquad G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\qquad \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad\qquad G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\bigr)\Bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \rEI{\rAI{3,8}}}
\end{tabproof}



\FormulaThmDeltaR[Dedekindscher Rekursionssatz]{%
  \begin{aligned}
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\\
    \vdash{}&\exists! G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl(
      G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\qquad\qquad\qquad\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,
      G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))
    \Bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\vdash \exists! G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl(G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\Bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f\dsep G\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl({}\\
      &\qquad G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\qquad \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad\qquad G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\bigr)\Bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\vdash \exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl(G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\Bigr)}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{4}{G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{5}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rA}

  \proofstep{6}{H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{7}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &H(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rA}

  \proofstep{5}{G(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rAEa{5}}

  \proofstep{5}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rAEb{5}}

  \proofstep{7}{H(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rAEa{7}}

  \proofstep{7}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rAEb{7}}

  \proofstep{4,5,6,7}{G=H}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))\vdash G=H}{4,6,8,10,9,11}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\exists! G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\,\Bigl({}\\
      &\qquad G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\qquad \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl({}\\
      &\qquad\qquad G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\bigr)\Bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \UEI{3,4,5,6,7,12}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsubsection{Die Rekursionsabbildung}

\paragraph{Definition der Rekursionsabbildung}

\FormulaDefDeltaR[Definition der Rekursionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash{}\\
    &\RecFun{m_0}{f}\coloneqq \iota G\Bigl({}\\
    &\qquad G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M \land{}\\
    &\qquad \bigl(
      G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
    &\qquad\qquad \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
      G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))
    \bigr)\bigr)
    \Bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}\coloneqq
  \iota G\Bigl(
    G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M \land
    \bigl(
      G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land
      \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
        G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))
      \bigr)
    \bigr)
  \Bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f\dsep G}%
}

\paragraph{Grundlegende Eigenschaften}

\FormulaThmDelta[Die Rekursionsabbildung ist eine Abbildung]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \rAEa{\FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}\coloneqq
  \iota G\Bigl(
    G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M \land
    \bigl(
      G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land
      \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
        G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))
      \bigr)
    \bigr)
  \Bigr)}{1,2}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Werte der Rekursionsabbildung liegen in $M$]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\in M%
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep m_0\dsep n}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep a\in A\vdash F(a)\in B}{4,3}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Anfangswert der Rekursionsabbildung]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
        \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
      \bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}\coloneqq
  \iota G\Bigl(
    G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M \land
    \bigl(
      G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land
      \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
        G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))
      \bigr)
    \bigr)
  \Bigr)}{1,2}}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{\rAEa{3}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Rekursionsgleichung der Rekursionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\\
    &\vdash \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0 \land{}\\
      &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
        \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
      \bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \rAEb{\FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}\coloneqq
  \iota G\Bigl(
    G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M \land
    \bigl(
      G(\varnothing)=m_0 \land
      \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
        G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))
      \bigr)
    \bigr)
  \Bigr)}{1,2}}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
    \bigr)
  }{\rAEb{4}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{%
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
  }{\rRE{\rUE{5},3}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Rekursionsgleichung der Rekursionsabbildung für Nichtnullstellen]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\neq\varnothing\\
    &\vdash \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\neq\varnothing\vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep k\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{n\neq\varnothing}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[3,4]{%
    \exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n=\Succ(k)\bigr)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in\mathbb{N}\dsep x\neq \varnothing\vdash \exists y\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(x=\Succ(y)\bigr)}{3,4}}

  \proofstepwidestar[6]{k\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[7]{n=\Succ(k)}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[6]{\Pred(\Succ(k))=k}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Pred(\Succ(n))=n}{6}}

  \proofstepwidestar[3,6,7]{\Pred(n)=k}{\rIE{7,8}}
  \proofstepwidestar[3,6,7]{k=\Pred(n)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{9}}

  \proofstepwide[1,2,3,4,6,7]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(k))}{\rIE{7}}

  \proofstepwide[1,2,3,4,6,7]{}{=}{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k))}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
    }{1,2,6}}

  \proofstepwide[1,2,3,4,6,7]{}{=}{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))}{\rIE{10}}

  \proofstepwide[1,2,3,4,6,7]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)}{=}{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))}{\rChain{11,12,13}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{%
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))
  }{%
    \rEE{5,6,7,14}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\FormulaThmDeltaR{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\neq\varnothing\\
    &\vdash f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\neq\varnothing\vdash
  f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{n\neq\varnothing}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{%
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\neq\varnothing\vdash
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))
    }{1,2,3,4}}
  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{%
    f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{5}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\paragraph{Zusammenhang mit dem Rekursionskern}

\FormulaThmDelta[Rekursionsabbildung und Rekursionskern stimmen überein]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}=\RecCore{m_0}{f}
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f\dsep G\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{ m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecCore{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{1,2}}

  \proofstep{7}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2,7}{%
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))}{1,2,7}}

  \proofstep{1,2,7}{%
    \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \RecCore{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n))}{1,2,7}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{%
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)=\RecCore{m_0}{f}(n)
    \bigr)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      G\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep H\colon \mathbb{N}\to M\dsep
      G(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep H(\varnothing)=m_0\dsep
      \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,G(\Succ(n))=f(G(n))\dsep
      \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,H(\Succ(n))=f(H(n))
      \vdash G=H
    }{3,4,5,6,8,9}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}=\RecCore{m_0}{f}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\forall x\in A (F(x)=G(x)) \eqvdash F=G}{10}}
\end{tabproof}


\paragraph{Hilfssätze zur Injektivität der Rekursionsabbildung}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Nullfall des Induktionsschritts für die Rekursionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep{}\\
    &\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\dsep{}\\
    &u\in\mathbb{N}\dsep k\in\mathbb{N}\dsep{}\\
    &\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))\vdash k\neq\varnothing
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep
  \forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\dsep
  u\in\mathbb{N}\dsep k\in\mathbb{N}\dsep
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))\vdash k\neq\varnothing
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep u\dsep k\dsep x\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\to M}{\FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{2}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[5]{u\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{k\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[7]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,5]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u)\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\in M}{1,3,5}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u))\neq m_0}{%
    \rRE{\rUE{4},8}}

  \proofstepwidestar[10]{k=\varnothing}{\rA}

  \proofstepwide[1,2,5]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u))}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{%
        m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
        \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
      }{1,3,5}}}
  \proofstepwide[7]{}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{7}}
  \proofstepwide[10]{}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)}{\rIE{10}}
  \proofstepwide[1,2]{}{=}{m_0}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\vdash
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{1,3}}
  \proofstepwide[1,2,5,7,10]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u))}{=}{m_0}{\rChain{11,12,13,14}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,7,10]{\bot}{\rBI{9,15}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,7]{k\neq\varnothing}{\rCI{10,16}}
\end{tabproofwide}


\FormulaThmDeltaR[Hilfssatz zum Induktionsanfang der Eindeutigkeit der Rekursionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep{}\\
    &\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\dsep{}\\
    &k\in\mathbb{N}\dsep
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)\vdash k=\varnothing
  \end{aligned}

  \forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\dsep

  \RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)\vdash k=\varnothing

  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproofwide}

  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\inj M}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[5]{k\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[6]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[7]{k\neq\varnothing}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[5]{\Pred(k)\in\mathbb{N}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Pred(n)\in\mathbb{N}}{5}}

    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\in M}{1,3,8}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k)))\neq m_0}{%
    \rRE{\rUE{4},9}}

  \proofstepwide[1,2,5,7]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k)))}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\neq\varnothing\vdash

  \proofstepwide[6]{}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwide[1,2]{}{=}{m_0}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)=m_0}{1,3}}
  \proofstepwide[1,2,5,6,7]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k)))}{=}{m_0}{\rChain{11,12,13}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,6,7]{\bot}{\rBI{10,14}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,6]{k=\varnothing}{\rCE{7,15}}
\end{tabproofwide}


\FormulaThmDeltaR[Hilfssatz zum Induktionsschritt der Eindeutigkeit der Rekursionsabbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep{}\\
    &\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\dsep{}\\
    &u\in\mathbb{N}\dsep{}\\
    &\forall x\in\mathbb{N}\,\Bigl(
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(x)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u)\rightarrow x=u
    \Bigr)\dsep{}\\
    &k\in\mathbb{N}\dsep
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))\vdash k=\Succ(u)
  \end{aligned}

}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep u\dsep k\dsep x\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproofwide}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\to M}{\FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{2}}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[5]{u\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]

          \RecFun{m_0}{f}(x)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u)\\
        &\rightarrow x=u
        \Bigr)
      \end{aligned}
    }{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[7]{k\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[8]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))}{\rA}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,7,8]{k\neq\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep
      \forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\dsep

      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))\vdash k\neq\varnothing
    }{1,2,4,5,7,8}}

  \proofstepwidestar[7]{\Pred(k)\in\mathbb{N}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Pred(n)\in\mathbb{N}}{7}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,5]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u)\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\in M}{1,3,5}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,7]{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k))\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\in M}{1,3,10}}

  \proofstepwide[1,2,4,5,7,8]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k)))}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\neq\varnothing\vdash
      f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(n)))=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)
    }{1,3,7,9}}
  \proofstepwide[8]{}{=}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(u))}{\FormulaRefAuto{P\vdash P}{8}}
  \proofstepwide[1,2,5]{}{=}{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u))}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
    }{1,3,5}}
  \proofstepwide[1,2,4,5,7,8]{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k)))}{=}{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u))}{\rChain{13,14,15}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,7,8]{%
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k))=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{2,12,11,16}}

    \proofstepwidestar[6,10]{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]
        &\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Pred(k))=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(u)\\
        &\rightarrow \Pred(k)=u
      \end{aligned}
    }{\rRE{\rUE{6},10}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,6,7,8]{\Pred(k)=u}{\rRE{17,18}}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,4,5,6,7,8]{k=\Succ(u)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{k\in\mathbb{N}\dsep k\neq\varnothing\dsep \Pred(k)=n\vdash k=\Succ(n)}{7,9,19}}
\end{tabproofwide}

\proofpartwideindR[Induktionsschritt]{%

\proofpartwide{Schluss}
  \proofstepwidestar[1]{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[2]{f\colon M\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[3]{\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstepwidestar[4]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

      &\rightarrow k=n
      \Bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \makecell[l]{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{P(\varnothing)\dsep [x\in\mathbb{N},P(x)]\vdots P(\Succ(x))\dsep n\in\mathbb{N} \vdash P(n)}(%
      \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{%
        m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep
        \forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\vdash
        \forall k\in\mathbb{N}\,\Bigl(
          \RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\varnothing)\rightarrow

        m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep

      \\ )%
    }%
  }

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5]{%

      &\rightarrow k=n
    \end{aligned}

  \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,6]{k=n}{\rRE{6,8}}

\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\FormulaThmDelta[Die Rekursionsabbildung ist injektiv]{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep
  \forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\vdash
  \RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep x\dsep y\dsep z\dsep n\dsep k\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M
    }{1,2}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      \forall x\in\mathbb{N}\,\forall y\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
      &\RecFun{m_0}{f}(x)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(y)\\
      &\rightarrow x=y
      \bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep
      \forall z\in M\,\bigl(f(z)\neq m_0\bigr)\dsep
      n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep k\in\mathbb{N}\dsep
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(k)=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\vdash k=n
    }{1,2,3}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{4,5}}
\end{tabproof}

\chapter{Endliche Mengen}

\section{Begriff der Endlichkeit}

\FormulaDefDelta[Begriff der endlichen Menge]{%
  \Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)
}{
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{\textbf{Neue Symbole}}{}
  \DeltaRow{Endlichkeit}{}
}

\section{Elementare Eigenschaften endlicher Mengen}

\FormulaThmDelta[Transport der Endlichkeit entlang der Gleichmächtigkeit]{%
  \Finite(M)\dsep M \EqCard N \vdash \Finite(N)%
}{
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep N\dsep n}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{M \EqCard N}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{1}}

  \proofstep{4}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{n \EqCard M}{\rAEb{4}}
  \proofstep{2,4}{n \EqCard N}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \dsep B \EqCard C \vdash A \EqCard C}{6,2}}
  \proofstep{2,4}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard N}{\rAI{5,7}}
  \proofstep{2,4}{\exists n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard N\bigr)}{\rEI{8}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\exists n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard N\bigr)}{\rEE{3,4,9}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Finite(N)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{10}}
\end{tabproof}

\paragraph{Explizite Bijektionen}

\FormulaThmDelta[Charakterisierung der Endlichkeit durch Bijektionen]{%
  \Finite(M)\vdash \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists F\colon n\bij M
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{1}}

  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{n \EqCard M}{\rAEb{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{\exists F\colon n\bij M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{5}}

  \proofstep{7}{F\colon n\bij M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3,7}{\exists F\colon n\bij M}{\rEI{7}}
  \proofstep{3,7}{\exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists F\colon n\bij M}{\rEI{\rAI{4,8}}}

  \proofstep{1}{\exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists F\colon n\bij M}{\rEE{2,3,9}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Transport der Endlichkeit mittels Bijektion]{%
  \Finite(M)\dsep F\colon M\bij N \vdash \Finite(N)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep N}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon M\bij N}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{M \EqCard N}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Finite(N)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\dsep M \EqCard N \vdash \Finite(N)}{1,3}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Transport der Endlichkeit mittels umgekehrter Bijektion]{%
  \Finite(M)\dsep F\colon N\bij M \vdash \Finite(N)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep N}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon N\bij M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{N \EqCard M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{M \EqCard N}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \vdash B \EqCard A}{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Finite(N)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\dsep M \EqCard N \vdash \Finite(N)}{1,4}}
\end{tabproof}

\section{Beispiele endlicher Mengen}

\subsection{Adjunktion eines neuen Elements}

\FormulaThmDelta[Typisierung der vorangestellten Inklusionsabbildung]{%
  F\colon n\bij A \vdash \iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{F\colon n\to A}{\FormulaRefAuto{Bijektive Funktion}{1}}
  \proofstep{}{A\subseteq A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq A\cup B}}
  \proofstep{1}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\subseteq C \dsep F\colon A\to B \vdash \iota_{B,C}\circ F\colon A\to C}{3,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Werte der vorangestellten Inklusionsabbildung]{%
  F\colon n\bij A \dsep u\in n \vdash
  \iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F(u)=F(u)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep u}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{u\in n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{F\colon n\to A}{\FormulaRefAuto{Bijektive Funktion}{1}}
  \proofstep{2}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F(u)=\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}(F(u))}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A \vdash (F\circ G)(x)=F(G(x))}{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{F(u)\in A}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{3,2}}
  \proofstep{}{A\subseteq A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq A\cup B}}
  \proofstep{5}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}(F(u))=F(u)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \dsep x\in A \vdash \iota_{A,B}(x)=x}{6,5}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F(u)=F(u)}{\rIE{4,7}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Werte der adjungierten Abbildung auf alten Punkten]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep u\in n \vdash
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=F(u)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep u}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{u\in n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon n\bij A \vdash \iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\in A\cup\{a\}}}
  \proofstep{1}{n\notin n}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\notin n}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F(u)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep f\colon A\to M \dsep b\in M \vdash \forall x\in A\,\ExtMap{f}{a}{b}(x)=f(x)}{6,4,5}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F(u)=F(u)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon n\bij A \dsep u\in n \vdash \iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F(u)=F(u)}{2,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=F(u)}{\rIE{7,8}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Wert der adjungierten Abbildung am neuen Punkt]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(n)=a
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon n\bij A \vdash \iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\in A\cup\{a\}}}
  \proofstep{1}{n\notin n}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\notin n}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(n)=a}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep f\colon A\to M \dsep b\in M \vdash \ExtMap{f}{a}{b}(a)=b}{5,3,4}}
\end{tabproof}



\FormulaThmDelta[Typisierung der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\to A\cup\{a\}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon n\bij A \vdash \iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F\colon n\to A\cup\{a\}}{2}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\in A\cup\{a\}}}
  \proofstep{1}{n\notin n}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\notin n}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\to A\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep f\colon A\to M \dsep b\in M \vdash \ExtMap{f}{a}{b}\colon (A\cup\{a\})\to M}{5,3,4}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Fall $x,y\in n$ der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\dsep y\in n\dsep{}\\
    &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
    &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\dsep y\in n\dsep
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{x\in n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{y\in n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
      &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\inj A}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F\colon A\inj B}{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=F(x)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep u\in n \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=F(u)}{1,2,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,4}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)=F(y)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep u\in n \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=F(u)}{1,2,4}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{F(x)=F(y)}{\rIE{7,\rIE{5,8}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{x=y}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektivität}{6,3,4,9}}
\end{tabproof}


\FormulaThmDeltaR[Fall $x\in n,\; y=n$ der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep{}\\
    &x\in n\dsep y=n\dsep{}\\
    &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
    &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\dsep y=n\dsep
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{x\in n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5}{y=n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
      &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rA}

  \proofstep{3}{F\colon n\to A}{\FormulaRefAuto{Bijektive Funktion}{3}}
  \proofstep{2,3,4}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=F(x)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep u\in n \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=F(u)}{2,3,4}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(n)=a}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(n)=a}{2,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4,5}{F(x)=a}{\rIE{8,\rIE{6,\rIE{5,9}}}}
  \proofstep{3,4}{F(x)\in A}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{7,4}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4,5}{a\in A}{\rIE{10,11}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4,5}{\bot}{\rBI{12,1}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4,5}{x=y}{\rCE{13}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Fall $x=n,\; y=n$ der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep x=n\dsep y=n\dsep{}\\
    &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
    &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep x=n\dsep y=n\dsep
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{x=n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{y=n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
      &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)
    \end{aligned}
  }{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n=y}{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{3}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{x=y}{\rIE{2,5}}
\end{tabproof}


\FormulaThmDelta[Injektivität der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &a\notin A \dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep{}\\
    &x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep{}\\
    &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
    &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Fall $x\in n$]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep{}\\
      &x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep x\in n\dsep{}\\
      &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
      &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep
    x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep x\in n\dsep
    \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=
    \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{a\notin A}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{x\in n\cup\{n\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in n\cup\{n\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{x\in n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]
        &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
        &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)
      \end{aligned}
    }{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in n\lor y=n}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cup\{a\} \vdash x\in A\lor x=a}{5}}

    \proofstepwidestar[9]{y\in n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,6,9]{x=y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\dsep y\in n\dsep \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y}{2,3,6,9,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[11]{y=n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,6,11]{x=y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\dsep y=n\dsep \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y}{1,2,3,6,11,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,5,6]{x=y}{\rOE{8,9,10,11,12}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Fall $x=n$]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep{}\\
      &x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep x=n\dsep{}\\
      &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
      &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep
    x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep x=n\dsep
    \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=
    \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{a\notin A}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{x\in n\cup\{n\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in n\cup\{n\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{x=n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]
        &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
        &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)
      \end{aligned}
    }{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in n\lor y=n}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cup\{a\} \vdash x\in A\lor x=a}{5}}

    \proofstepwidestar[9]{y\in n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]
        &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)= {}\\
        &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)
      \end{aligned}
    }{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,6,9]{y=x}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\dsep y=n\dsep \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y}{1,2,3,9,6,10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,6,9]{x=y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{11}}

    \proofstepwidestar[13]{y=n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,6,13]{x=y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep x=n\dsep y=n\dsep \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y}{2,6,13,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,5,6]{x=y}{\rOE{8,9,12,13,14}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{a\notin A}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{x\in n\cup\{n\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in n\cup\{n\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[6]{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]
        &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
        &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)
      \end{aligned}
    }{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[4]{x\in n\lor x=n}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cup\{a\} \vdash x\in A\lor x=a}{4}}

    \proofstepwidestar[8]{x\in n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,8]{x=y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep x\in n\dsep \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y}{1,2,3,4,5,8,6}}

    \proofstepwidestar[10]{x=n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5,10]{x=y}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep x=n\dsep \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y}{1,2,3,4,5,10,6}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,5]{x=y}{\rOE{7,8,9,10,11}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\FormulaThmDelta[Fall $z\in A$ der Surjektivität der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep z\in A \vdash
  \exists x\in n\cup\{n\}\,\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep z\dsep x}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{z\in A}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\sur A}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F\colon A\sur B}{2}}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\exists x\in n\,F(x)=z}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Surjektivität}{4,3}}

  \proofstep{6}{x\in n\land F(x)=z}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{x\in n}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstep{6}{F(x)=z}{\rAEb{6}}
  \proofstep{6}{x\in n\cup\{n\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{z\in A\vdash z\in A\cup B}{7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,6}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=F(x)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep u\in n \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=F(u)}{1,2,7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,6}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z}{\rIE{10,8}}
  \proofstep{1,2,6}{\exists u\in n\cup\{n\}\,\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=z}{%
    \rEI{\rAI{9,11}}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\exists u\in n\cup\{n\}\,\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=z}{%
    \rEE{5,6,12}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Fall $z=a$ der Surjektivität der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep z=a \vdash
  \exists x\in n\cup\{n\}\,\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep z}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{z=a}{\rA}

  \proofstep{}{n\in n\cup\{n\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\in A\cup\{a\}}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(n)=a}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(n)=a}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{3}{a=z}{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(n)=z}{\rIE{5,6}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\exists u\in n\cup\{n\}\,\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(u)=z}{\rEI{\rAI{4,7}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Surjektivität der adjungierten Abbildung]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &a\notin A \dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep z\in A\cup\{a\}\\
    &\vdash \exists x\in n\cup\{n\}\,
      \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z

  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}

      \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z

      \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z
    \end{aligned}
  }

    \proofstepwidestar[4]{z\in A\cup\{a\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{z\in A}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[2,3,5]{\exists x\in n\cup\{n\}\,\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z}{%

  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{a\notin A}{\rA}

      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cup\{a\} \vdash x\in A\lor x=a}{4}}

    \proofstepwidestar[6]{z\in A}{\rA}
