\paragraph{Bijektivität}
\FormulaThmDelta[Adjunktion einer Bijektion]{%
  a\notin A \dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash
  \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\bij (A\cup\{a\})
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep x\dsep y\dsep z}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\to A\cup\{a\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\to A\cup\{a\}}{2,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\inj (A\cup\{a\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{4,\FormulaRefAuto{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]
        &a\notin A \dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep{}\\
        &x\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep y\in n\cup\{n\}\dsep{}\\
        &\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)= {}\\
        &\qquad \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(y)\vdash x=y
      \end{aligned}
    }{1,2,3}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\sur (A\cup\{a\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Surjektive Funktion}{4,\FormulaRefAuto{%
      \begin{aligned}[t]
        &a\notin A \dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A\dsep z\in A\cup\{a\}\\
        &\vdash \exists x\in n\cup\{n\}\,
          \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}(x)=z
      \end{aligned}
    }{1,2,3}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{%
    \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\bij (A\cup\{a\})
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B\dsep F\colon A\sur B \vdash F\colon A\bij B}{5,6}}
\end{tabproof}
\paragraph{Erhaltung der Endlichkeit}


\FormulaThmDelta[Adjunktion eines neuen Elements erhält Endlichkeit]{%
  a\notin A \dsep \Finite(A) \vdash \Finite(A\cup\{a\})
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep n\dsep m}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\Finite(A)}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{\exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists F\colon n\bij A}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\vdash \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists F\colon n\bij M}{2}}

  \proofstep{4}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land \exists F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{\exists F\colon n\bij A}{\rAEb{4}}

  \proofstep{7}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,5,7}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\bij (A\cup\{a\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\bij (A\cup\{a\})}{1,5,7}}

  \proofstep{1,5,7}{\exists G\colon (n\cup\{n\})\bij (A\cup\{a\})}{\rEI{8}}
  \proofstep{1,5,7}{(n\cup\{n\}) \EqCard (A\cup\{a\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{9}}
  \proofstep{5}{(n\cup\{n\})\in\mathbb{N}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash (n\cup\{n\})\in\mathbb{N}}{5}}

  \proofstep{1,5,7}{\exists m\in \mathbb{N}\,m \EqCard (A\cup\{a\})}{%
    \rEI{\rAI{11,10}}}
  \proofstep{1,5,7}{\Finite(A\cup\{a\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{12}}

  \proofstep{1,4}{\Finite(A\cup\{a\})}{\rEE{6,7,13}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Finite(A\cup\{a\})}{\rEE{3,4,14}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Adjunktion endlich vieler Elemente}

\FormulaThmDelta[Das Bild der leeren Menge ist leer]{%
  F\colon A\to B \vdash F[\varnothing]=\varnothing
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep B\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{F\colon A\to B}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{y\in F[\varnothing]}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\exists x\in \varnothing\,y=F(x)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{2}}
  \proofstep{4}{x\in \varnothing \land y=F(x)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{x\in \varnothing}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{\bot}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in \varnothing \eqvdash \bot}{5}}
  \proofstep{4}{y\in \varnothing}{\rCE{6}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{y\in \varnothing}{\rEE{3,4,7}}
  \proofstep{1}{\forall y\,(y\in F[\varnothing]\rightarrow y\in \varnothing)}{\rUI{\rRI{2,8}}}
  \proofstep{1}{F[\varnothing]\subseteq \varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{9}}

  \proofstep{11}{y\in \varnothing}{\rA}
  \proofstep{11}{\bot}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in \varnothing \eqvdash \bot}{11}}
  \proofstep{11}{y\in F[\varnothing]}{\rCE{12}}
  \proofstep{1}{\forall y\,(y\in \varnothing \rightarrow y\in F[\varnothing])}{\rUI{\rRI{11,13}}}
  \proofstep{1}{\varnothing\subseteq F[\varnothing]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{14}}

  \proofstep{1}{F[\varnothing]=\varnothing}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B\dsep B\subseteq A \vdash A=B}{10,15}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Zerlegung des Bildes einer Nachfolgermenge]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash{}\\
    &F[\Succ(n)]=(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash F[\Succ(n)]=(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung \(F[\Succ(n)]\subseteq (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\)]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash{}\\
      &F[\Succ(n)]\subseteq (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash F[\Succ(n)]\subseteq (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{F\colon \Succ(n)\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\subseteq \Succ(n)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\subseteq \Succ(n)}{1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{F\restriction_n\colon n\to M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A \vdash F\restriction_C\colon C\to B}{3}}

    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2,5]{\exists x\in \Succ(n)\,y=F(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{5}}

    \proofstepwidestar[7]{x\in \Succ(n)\land y=F(x)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{x\in \Succ(n)}{\rAEa{7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[7]{y=F(x)}{\rAEb{7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\Succ(n)=n\cup\{n\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Succ(n)=n\cup\{n\}}{1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,7]{x\in n\cup\{n\}}{\rIE{8,10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,7]{x\in n\lor x=n}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cup\{a\} \vdash x\in A\lor x=a}{11}}

    \proofstepwidestar[13]{x\in n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4,13]{F\restriction_n(x)=F(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A \dsep x\in C \vdash F\restriction_C(x)=F(x)}{3,13}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4,13]{F(x)=F\restriction_n(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{14}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,7,13]{y=F\restriction_n(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{9,15}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,7,13]{\exists x\in n\,y=F\restriction_n(x)}{\rEI{\rAI{13,16}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\leftrightarrow \exists x\in n\,y=F\restriction_n(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4,7,13]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{P \leftrightarrow Q, Q \vdash P}{18,17}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4,7,13]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{z \in A \vdash z \in A \cup B}{19}}

    \proofstepwidestar[21]{x=n}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[21]{n=x}{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{21}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,7,21]{y=F(n)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x = y \dsep a = F(y) \vdash a = F(x)}{22,9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,7,21]{y\in \{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in \{a\}\eqvdash x=a}{23}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,7,21]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{z \in B \vdash z \in A \cup B}{24}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,7]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\rOE{12,13,20,21,25}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\forall y\,(y\in F[\Succ(n)]\rightarrow y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\})}{%
      \rUI{\rRI{5,26}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{F[\Succ(n)]\subseteq (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{27}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Teilmengenrichtung \((F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\subseteq F[\Succ(n)]\)]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash{}\\
      &(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\subseteq F[\Succ(n)]
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\subseteq F[\Succ(n)]
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{F\colon \Succ(n)\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\subseteq \Succ(n)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\subseteq \Succ(n)}{1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{F\restriction_n\colon n\to M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A \vdash F\restriction_C\colon C\to B}{3}}

    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[5]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\lor y=F(n)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cup\{a\} \vdash x\in A\lor x=a}{5}}

    \proofstepwidestar[7]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4]{y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\leftrightarrow \exists x\in n\,y=F\restriction_n(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4,7]{\exists x\in n\,y=F\restriction_n(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{P \leftrightarrow Q, P \vdash Q}{8,7}}
    \proofstepwidestar[10]{x\in n\land y=F\restriction_n(x)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[10]{x\in n}{\rAEa{10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[10]{y=F\restriction_n(x)}{\rAEb{10}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,10]{x\in \Succ(n)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B, x\in A \vdash x\in B}{3,11}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4,10]{F\restriction_n(x)=F(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A \dsep x\in C \vdash F\restriction_C(x)=F(x)}{3,11}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,4,10]{F(x)=F\restriction_n(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{14}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,10]{y=F(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{12,15}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,10]{\exists x\in \Succ(n)\,y=F(x)}{\rEI{\rAI{13,16}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{y\in F[\Succ(n)]\leftrightarrow \exists x\in \Succ(n)\,y=F(x)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,10]{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{P \leftrightarrow Q, Q \vdash P}{18,17}}

    \proofstepwidestar[20]{y=F(n)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in \Succ(n)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\in\Succ(n)}{1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,20]{\exists x\in \Succ(n)\,y=F(x)}{\rEI{\rAI{21,20}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,20]{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{P \leftrightarrow Q, Q \vdash P}{18,22}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{\rOE{6,7,19,20,23}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\forall y\,(y\in (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\rightarrow y\in F[\Succ(n)])}{%
      \rUI{\rRI{5,24}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\subseteq F[\Succ(n)]}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{25}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{F\colon \Succ(n)\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{F[\Succ(n)]\subseteq (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash F[\Succ(n)]\subseteq (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{1,2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\subseteq F[\Succ(n)]}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash (F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\subseteq F[\Succ(n)]}{1,2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{F[\Succ(n)]=(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B\dsep B\subseteq A \vdash A=B}{3,4}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}


\FormulaThmDeltaR[Adjunktion endlich vieler Elemente]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &\Finite(A)\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\to M \vdash{}\\
    &\Finite(A\cup F[n])
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  \Finite(A)\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\to M \vdash \Finite(A\cup F[n])
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep M\dsep n\dsep k}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideind[Induktionsanfang]{%
    \Finite(A)\vdash \forall F\,\bigl(F\colon \varnothing\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\varnothing])\bigr)}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\Finite(A)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{F\colon \varnothing\to M}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{F[\varnothing]=\varnothing}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B \vdash F[\varnothing]=\varnothing}{2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{F[\varnothing]\cup A=\varnothing\cup A}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A=B\vdash A\cup C = B\cup C}{3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{A\cup F[\varnothing]=F[\varnothing]\cup A}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \cup B = B \cup A}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\varnothing\cup A=A}{\FormulaRefAuto{A = \varnothing \cup A}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{A\cup F[\varnothing]=A}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{5,\FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{4,6}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\Finite(A\cup F[\varnothing])}{\rIE{7,1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{F\colon \varnothing\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\varnothing])}{\rII{2,8}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\forall F\,\bigl(F\colon \varnothing\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\varnothing])\bigr)}{\rUI{\rRI{2,9}}}
  \closeproofpartwideind

  \proofpartwideindR[Induktionsschritt]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &\Finite(A)\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep
      \forall G\,\bigl(G\colon n\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup G[n])\bigr)\vdash{}\\
      &\forall F\,\bigl(F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\Succ(n)])\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    \Finite(A)\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall G\,\bigl(G\colon n\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup G[n])\bigr)\vdash \forall F\,\bigl(F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\Succ(n)])\bigr)
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\Finite(A)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{\forall G\,\bigl(G\colon n\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup G[n])\bigr)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{F\colon \Succ(n)\to M}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[2]{n\subseteq \Succ(n)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\subseteq \Succ(n)}{2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[4,5]{F\restriction_n\colon n\to M}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A \vdash F\restriction_C\colon C\to B}{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{F\restriction_n\colon n\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup (F\restriction_n)[n])}{\rUE{3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{\Finite(A\cup (F\restriction_n)[n])}{\rIE{6,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[2,4]{F[\Succ(n)]=(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \vdash F[\Succ(n)]=(F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{2,4}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{F[\Succ(n)]\cup A=\bigl((F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\bigr)\cup A}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A=B\vdash A\cup C = B\cup C}{9}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{A\cup F[\Succ(n)]=F[\Succ(n)]\cup A}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \cup B = B \cup A}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{\bigl((F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\bigr)\cup A=A\cup\bigl((F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\bigr)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \cup B = B \cup A}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{A\cup F[\Succ(n)]=A\cup\bigl((F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\bigr)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{11,\FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{10,12}}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{A\cup\bigl((F\restriction_n)[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\bigr)=(A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n])\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A \cup (B \cup C) = (A \cup B) \cup C}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{A\cup F[\Succ(n)]=(A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n])\cup\{F(n)\}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{13,14}}

    \proofstepwidestar[]{F(n)\in A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n]\lor F(n)\notin A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n]}{\FormulaRefAuto{P\lor \neg P}}

    \proofstepwidestar[17]{F(n)\in A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n]}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[17]{(A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n])\cup\{F(n)\}=A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n]}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\cup \{a\}=A\eqvdash a\in A}{17}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,17]{\Finite((A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n])\cup\{F(n)\})}{%
      \rIE{18,8}}

    \proofstepwidestar[20]{F(n)\notin A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n]}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4,20]{\Finite((A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n])\cup\{F(n)\})}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep \Finite(A) \vdash \Finite(A\cup\{a\})}{20,8}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{\Finite((A\cup(F\restriction_n)[n])\cup\{F(n)\})}{\rOE{16,17,19,20,21}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{\Finite(A\cup F[\Succ(n)])}{\rIE{15,22}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\Succ(n)])}{\rII{4,23}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\forall F\,\bigl(F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\Succ(n)])\bigr)}{\rUI{\rRI{4,24}}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Induktionsschluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\Finite(A)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{F\colon n\to M}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\forall k\in\mathbb{N}\,\forall G\,\bigl(G\colon k\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup G[k])\bigr)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{P(\varnothing)\dsep \forall k\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(P(k)\rightarrow P(\Succ(k))\bigr)\vdash \forall k\in\mathbb{N}\,P(k)}{%
        \FormulaRefAuto{\forall F\,\bigl(F\colon \varnothing\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\varnothing])\bigr)}{1},%
        \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(A)\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall G\,\bigl(G\colon n\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup G[n])\bigr)\vdash \forall F\,\bigl(F\colon \Succ(n)\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[\Succ(n)])\bigr)}{1,2},%
        2}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\forall G\,\bigl(G\colon n\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup G[n])\bigr)}{\rUE{4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{F\colon n\to M \rightarrow \Finite(A\cup F[n])}{\rUE{5}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\Finite(A\cup F[n])}{\rIE{3,6}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\subsection{Teilmengen natürlicher Zahlen sind endlich}

\FormulaThmDelta[Die leere Menge ist endlich]{%
  \Finite(\varnothing)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{\varnothing\in\mathbb{N}}{\FormulaRefAuto{\varnothing\in\mathbb{N}}}
  \proofstep{}{\varnothing \EqCard \varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard A}}
  \proofstep{}{\varnothing\in\mathbb{N}\land \varnothing \EqCard \varnothing}{\rAI{1,2}}
  \proofstep{}{\exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,n \EqCard \varnothing}{\rEI{3}}
  \proofstep{}{\Finite(\varnothing)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{4}}
\end{tabproof}



\FormulaThmDelta[Induktionsanfang für endliche Teilmengen natürlicher Zahlen]{%
  C\subseteq \varnothing \vdash \Finite(C)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{C}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{C\subseteq \varnothing}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{C=\varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq \varnothing \vdash A=\varnothing}{1}}
  \proofstep{}{\Finite(\varnothing)}{\FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(\varnothing)}}
  \proofstep{1}{\varnothing=C}{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b \vdash b=a}{2}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(C)}{\rIE{4,3}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Fall \(n\in C\) im Induktionsschritt für endliche Teilmengen natürlicher Zahlen]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep{}\\
    &C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\in C \vdash \Finite(C)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n\dsep C}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{C\subseteq \Succ(n)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{n\in C}{\rA}

  \proofstep{}{C\cap n\subseteq n}{\FormulaRefAuto{A\cap B \subseteq B}}
  \proofstep{2}{(C\cap n)\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C\cap n)}{\rUE{2}}
  \proofstep{2}{\Finite(C\cap n)}{\rRE{5,6}}

  \proofstep{8}{n\in C\cap n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{8}{n\in n}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cap B\vdash x\in B}{8}}
  \proofstep{1,8}{\bot}{\rBI{9,\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\notin n}{1}}}
  \proofstep{1}{n\notin C\cap n}{\rCI{8,10}}

  \proofstep{1,2,4}{\Finite((C\cap n)\cup\{n\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep \Finite(A) \vdash \Finite(A\cup\{a\})}{11,7}}
  \proofstep{1,3,4}{C=(C\cap n)\cup\{n\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep B\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\in B \vdash B=(B\cap n)\cup\{n\}}{1,3,4}}
  \proofstep{1,3,4}{(C\cap n)\cup\{n\}=C}{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b \vdash b=a}{13}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{\Finite(C)}{\rIE{14,12}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Fall \(n\notin C\) im Induktionsschritt für endliche Teilmengen natürlicher Zahlen]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep{}\\
    &C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\notin C \vdash \Finite(C)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n\dsep C}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{C\subseteq \Succ(n)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{n\notin C}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,3,4}{C\subseteq n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep B\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\notin B \vdash B\subseteq n}{1,3,4}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)}{\rUE{2}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{\Finite(C)}{\rIE{5,6}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Induktionsschritt für endliche Teilmengen natürlicher Zahlen]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep C\subseteq \Succ(n)\vdash
  \Finite(C)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n\dsep C}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideindR[Fall \(n\in C\)]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep{}\\
      &C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\in C \vdash \Finite(C)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep
    C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\in C \vdash \Finite(C)
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{C\subseteq \Succ(n)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{n\in C}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{\Finite(C)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{%
        \begin{aligned}[t]
          &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep{}\\
          &C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\in C \vdash \Finite(C)
        \end{aligned}
      }{1,2,3,4}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwideindR[Fall \(n\notin C\)]{%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep{}\\
      &C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\notin C \vdash \Finite(C)
    \end{aligned}
  }{%
    n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep
    C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\notin C \vdash \Finite(C)
  }
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[3]{C\subseteq \Succ(n)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[4]{n\notin C}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,4]{\Finite(C)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{%
        \begin{aligned}[t]
          &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep{}\\
          &C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\notin C \vdash \Finite(C)
        \end{aligned}
      }{1,2,3,4}}
  \closeproofpartwideindR

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[3]{C\subseteq \Succ(n)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[]{n\in C \lor n\notin C}{\FormulaRefAuto{P \lor \neg P}}

    \proofstepwidestar[5]{n\in C}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,5]{\Finite(C)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{%
        n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep
        C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\in C \vdash \Finite(C)
      }{1,2,3,5}}

    \proofstepwidestar[7]{n\notin C}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3,7]{\Finite(C)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{%
        n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep
        C\subseteq \Succ(n)\dsep n\notin C \vdash \Finite(C)
      }{1,2,3,7}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\Finite(C)}{\rOE{4,5,6,7,8}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\FormulaThmDelta[Teilmengen natürlicher Zahlen sind endlich als Allsatz]{%
  \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n\dsep C}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{}{%
    \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \varnothing \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \varnothing \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}}

  \proofstep{}{%
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\Bigl(
      \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)
      \rightarrow
      \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \Succ(n) \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)
    \Bigr)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\Bigl(
        \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)
        \rightarrow
        \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \Succ(n) \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)
      \Bigr)
    }}

  \proofstep{}{%
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P(\varnothing)\dsep \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(P(n)\rightarrow P(\Succ(n))\bigr)\vdash \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,P(n)}{1,2}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Teilmengen natürlicher Zahlen sind endlich]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep C\subseteq n \vdash \Finite(C)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n\dsep C}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideind[Induktionsanfang]{%
    \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \varnothing \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{C\subseteq \varnothing}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\Finite(C)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq \varnothing \vdash \Finite(C)}{1}}
    \proofstepwidestar[]{C\subseteq \varnothing \rightarrow \Finite(C)}{\rII{1,2}}
    \proofstepwidestar[]{%
      \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \varnothing \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{%
      \rUI{\rRI{1,3}}}
  \closeproofpartwideind

  \proofpartwideind[Induktionsschritt]{%
    n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\vdash
    \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \Succ(n) \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[3]{C\subseteq \Succ(n)}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2,3]{\Finite(C)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\dsep C\subseteq \Succ(n)\vdash \Finite(C)}{1,2,3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{C\subseteq \Succ(n)\rightarrow \Finite(C)}{\rII{3,4}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{%
      \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \Succ(n) \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{%
      \rUI{\rRI{3,5}}}
  \closeproofpartwideind

  \proofpartwide{Induktionsschluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{C\subseteq n}{\rA}

    \proofstepwidestar[1]{%
      \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{P(\varnothing)\dsep [x\in\mathbb{N},P(x)]\vdots P(\Succ(x))\dsep n\in\mathbb{N} \vdash P(n)}{%
        \FormulaRefAuto{\forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \varnothing \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)},%
        \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)\vdash \forall C\,\bigl(C\subseteq \Succ(n) \rightarrow \Finite(C)\bigr)},%
        1}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1]{C\subseteq n \rightarrow \Finite(C)}{\rUE{3}}
    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\Finite(C)}{\rIE{2,4}}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}



\subsection{Teilmengen endlicher Mengen sind endlich}

\FormulaThmDelta[Teilmengen endlicher Mengen sind endlich]{%
  T\subseteq M\dsep \Finite(M) \vdash \Finite(T)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{T\dsep M\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{T\subseteq M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\Finite(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists F\colon n\bij M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\vdash \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists F\colon n\bij M}{2}}
  \proofstep{4}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land \exists F\colon n\bij M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{\exists F\colon n\bij M}{\rAEb{4}}
  \proofstep{7}{F\colon n\bij M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,7}{F^{-1}[T]\subseteq n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq B\dsep F\colon A\bij B \vdash F^{-1}[C]\subseteq A}{1,7}}
  \proofstep{1,4,7}{\Finite(F^{-1}[T])}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep B\subseteq n \vdash \Finite(B)}{5,8}}
  \proofstep{1,7}{F\restriction_{F^{-1}[T]}\colon F^{-1}[T]\bij T}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \dsep T\subseteq B \vdash F\restriction_{F^{-1}[T]}\colon F^{-1}[T]\bij T}{7,1}}
  \proofstep{1,4,7}{\Finite(T)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\dsep F\colon M\bij N \vdash \Finite(N)}{9,10}}
  \proofstep{1,4}{\Finite(T)}{\rEE{6,7,11}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\Finite(T)}{\rEE{3,4,12}}
\end{tabproof}


\subsection{Hilfssatz: Bilder endlicher Mengen sind endlich}

\FormulaThmDelta[Bilder endlicher Mengen sind endlich]{%
  C\subseteq A\dsep F\colon A\to B\dsep \Finite(C) \vdash \Finite(F[C])
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep B\dsep C}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{C\subseteq A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon A\to B}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\Finite(C)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{F\restriction_C\colon C\sur F[C]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A \vdash F\restriction_C\colon C\twoheadrightarrow F[C]}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\exists G\colon F[C]\inj C}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\sur B\vdash \exists G\colon B\inj A}{4}}
  \proofstep{6}{G\colon F[C]\inj C}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{G\colon F[C]\bij G[F[C]]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B \vdash F\colon A\bij F[A]}{6}}
  \proofstep{6}{G\colon F[C]\to C}{\FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{6}}
  \proofstep{6}{G[F[C]]\subseteq C}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B \vdash F[A]\subseteq B}{8}}
  \proofstep{3,6}{\Finite(G[F[C]])}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{T\subseteq M\dsep \Finite(M) \vdash \Finite(T)}{9,3}}
  \proofstep{3,6}{\Finite(F[C])}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\dsep F\colon M\bij N \vdash \Finite(N)}{10,7}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\Finite(F[C])}{\rEE{5,6,11}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Disjunkte Vereinigungen endlicher Mengen sind endlich}

\FormulaThmDelta[Bild der leeren Menge]{%
  F[\varnothing]=\varnothing
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep B\dsep x}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{x\in F[\varnothing]}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists y\in\varnothing\,x=F(y)}{\FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{1}}
  \proofstep{3}{y\in\varnothing \land x=F(y)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{y\in\varnothing}{\rAEa{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{\bot}{\rBI{4,\FormulaRefAuto{x\notin\varnothing}{}}}
  \proofstep{1}{\bot}{\rEE{2,3,5}}
  \proofstep{}{x\notin F[\varnothing]}{\rCI{1,6}}
  \proofstep{}{\forall x\,\bigl(x\notin F[\varnothing]\bigr)}{\rUI{7}}
  \proofstep{}{F[\varnothing]=\varnothing}{\FormulaRefAuto{\forall x\, x\notin A\vdash A=\varnothing}{8}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Bild einer Nachfolgermenge]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to B \vdash F[\Succ(n)]=F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{B\dsep n\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon \Succ(n)\to B}{\rA}

  \proofstep{3}{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\exists x\in \Succ(n)\,y=F(x)}{\FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{3}}
  \proofstep{5}{x\in \Succ(n)\land y=F(x)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5}{x\in \Succ(n)}{\rAEa{5}}
  \proofstep{1,5}{x\in n\lor x=n}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\cup\{a\} \vdash x\in A\lor x=a}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Succ(n)=n\cup\{n\}}{1},6}}

  \proofstep{8}{x\in n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5,8}{y=F(x)}{\rAEb{5}}
  \proofstep{5,8}{y\in F[n]}{\FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{\rEI{\rAI{8,9}}}}
  \proofstep{5,8}{y\in F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{z\in A\vdash z\in A\cup B}{10}}

  \proofstep{12}{x=n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5,12}{y=F(n)}{\rAEb{5}}
  \proofstep{5,12}{y\in\{F(n)\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{x=a\vdash x\in\{a\}}{13}}
  \proofstep{5,12}{y\in F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{z\in B\vdash z\in A\cup B}{14}}

  \proofstep{3}{y\in F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\rEE{4,5,\rOE{7,8,11,12,15}}}
  \proofstep{}{F[\Succ(n)]\subseteq F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{3,16}}}}

  \proofstep{18}{y\in F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{18}{y\in F[n]\lor y\in\{F(n)\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{z\in A\cup B \eqvdash z\in A\lor z\in B}{18}}

  \proofstep{20}{y\in F[n]}{\rA}
  \proofstep{20}{\exists x\in n\,y=F(x)}{\FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{20}}
  \proofstep{22}{x\in n\land y=F(x)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{22}{x\in n}{\rAEa{22}}
  \proofstep{1,22}{x\in \Succ(n)}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\vdash x\in A\cup B}{23}}
  \proofstep{22}{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{\FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{\rEI{\rAI{24,\rAEb{22}}}}}
  \proofstep{20}{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{\rEE{21,22,25}}

  \proofstep{27}{y\in\{F(n)\}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{27}{y=F(n)}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in\{a\}\eqvdash x=a}{27}}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in \Succ(n)}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\vdash x\in A\cup B}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\in n\cup\{n\}}{1}}}
  \proofstep{27}{y\in F[\Succ(n)]}{\FormulaRefAuto{y\in F[A]\eqvdash \exists x\in A\,y=F(x)}{\rEI{\rAI{29,28}}}}

  \proofstep{}{F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}\subseteq F[\Succ(n)]}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B \coloneq \forall x\,(x\in A \rightarrow x\in B)}{\rUI{\rRI{18,\rOE{19,20,26,27,30}}}}}
  \proofstep{}{F[\Succ(n)]=F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B, B \subseteq A \vdash A = B}{17,31}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Disjunkte Vereinigungen endlicher Mengen sind endlich]{%
  A\cap B=\varnothing \dsep \Finite(A)\dsep \Finite(B) \vdash \Finite(A\cup B)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep B\dsep n\dsep m\dsep u\dsep k}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G\dsep H\dsep J}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{A\cap B=\varnothing}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{\Finite(A)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\Finite(B)}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{\exists n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n\EqCard A\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{2}}
  \proofstep{3}{\exists m\,\bigl(m\in\mathbb{N}\land m\EqCard B\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{3}}

  \proofstep{6}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land n\EqCard A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{7}{m\in\mathbb{N}\land m\EqCard B}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstep{6}{n\EqCard A}{\rAEb{6}}
  \proofstep{7}{m\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{7}}
  \proofstep{7}{m\EqCard B}{\rAEb{7}}
  \proofstep{6}{\exists F\colon n\bij A}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{9}}
  \proofstep{7}{\exists G\colon m\bij B}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{11}}

  \proofstep{13}{F\colon n\bij A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{14}{G\colon m\bij B}{\rA}

  \proofstep{10,13,14}{\exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[\varnothing])}{%
    \rEI{\rAI{8,\rIE{\FormulaRefAuto{Bild der leeren Menge},13}}}}

  \proofstep{16}{u\in\mathbb{N}\land \exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[u])}{\rA}
  \proofstep{16}{u\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{16}}
  \proofstep{16}{\exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[u])}{\rAEb{16}}

  \proofstep{19}{k\in\mathbb{N}\land \exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[u])}{\rA}
  \proofstep{19}{k\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{19}}
  \proofstep{19}{\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[u])}{\rAEb{19}}

  \proofstep{22}{H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[u])}{\rA}

  \proofstep{10,14,17}{G(u)\in B}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{\FormulaRefAuto{Bijektive Funktion}{14},17}}
  \proofstep{1,23}{G(u)\notin A}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\in B\dsep A\cap B=\varnothing \vdash x\notin A}{23,1}}
  \proofstep{10,14,17}{G(u)\notin G[u]}{\FormulaRefAuto{u\in\mathbb{N}\dsep G\colon \Succ(u)\inj B \vdash G(u)\notin G[u]}{17,\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F\colon A\inj B}{14}}}
  \proofstep{1,23,25}{G(u)\notin A\cup G[u]}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A\dsep a\notin B \vdash a\notin A\cup B}{24,25}}

  \proofstep{20,22,26}{\ExtMap{\iota_{A\cup G[u],(A\cup G[u])\cup\{G(u)\}}\circ H}{k}{G(u)}\colon \Succ(k)\bij ((A\cup G[u])\cup\{G(u)\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\bij A \vdash \ExtMap{\iota_{A,A\cup\{a\}}\circ F}{n}{a}\colon (n\cup\{n\})\bij (A\cup\{a\})}{26,20,22}}

  \proofstep{10,14,17}{G[\Succ(u)]=G[u]\cup\{G(u)\}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon \Succ(n)\to B \vdash F[\Succ(n)]=F[n]\cup\{F(n)\}}{17,\FormulaRefAuto{Bijektive Funktion}{14}}}
  \proofstep{20,22,26}{((A\cup G[u])\cup\{G(u)\})=A\cup G[\Succ(u)]}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b \vdash c\cup a = c\cup b}{27}}

  \proofstep{16,19,22}{\exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists J\colon k\bij (A\cup G[\Succ(u)])}{%
    \rEI{\rAI{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Succ(n)\in\mathbb{N}}{20},\rEI{\rIE{28,27}}}}}

  \proofstep{16}{u\in\mathbb{N}\rightarrow \bigl(\exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[u]) \rightarrow \exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists J\colon k\bij (A\cup G[\Succ(u)])\bigr)}{\rRI{17,\rII{18,29}}}

  \proofstep{10,13,14}{\forall u\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[u])}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P(\varnothing)\dsep \forall u\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(P(u)\rightarrow P(\Succ(u))\bigr)\vdash \forall u\in\mathbb{N}\,P(u)}{15,30}}

  \proofstep{10,13,14}{\exists k\in\mathbb{N}\,\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[m])}{\rRE{31,10}}
  \proofstep{10,14}{G[m]=B}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F[A]=B}{14}}

  \proofstep{33}{k\in\mathbb{N}\land \exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[m])}{\rA}
  \proofstep{33}{k\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{33}}
  \proofstep{33}{\exists H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[m])}{\rAEb{33}}
  \proofstep{36}{H\colon k\bij (A\cup G[m])}{\rA}
  \proofstep{33,36}{A\cup G[m] \EqCard A\cup B}{\FormulaRefAuto{A=B \vdash A\EqCard B}{\rIE{32}}}
  \proofstep{33,36}{\Finite(A\cup B)}{\FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\dsep M \EqCard N \vdash \Finite(N)}{\rAI{34,\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard A}{37}},38}}

  \proofstep{10,13,14,33}{\Finite(A\cup B)}{\rEE{35,36,39}}
  \proofstep{10,13}{\Finite(A\cup B)}{\rEE{32,33,40}}
  \proofstep{6,7,13}{\Finite(A\cup B)}{\rEE{12,14,41}}
  \proofstep{6,7}{\Finite(A\cup B)}{\rEE{13,14,42}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\Finite(A\cup B)}{\rEE{4,6,\rEE{5,7,43}}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Potenzmengen endlicher Mengen sind endlich}

\FormulaDefDelta[Funktionsvorschrift der Potenzmengen-Adjunktion]{%
  a\notin A \dsep X\in \powerset(A) \vdash t_{J_{A,a}}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{J_{A,a}}}
}

\FormulaThmDelta[Typisierung von \(J_{A,a}\)]{%
  a\notin A \dsep X\in \powerset(A) \vdash t_{J_{A,a}}(X)\in \powerset(A\cup\{a\})
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{J_{A,a}}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in \powerset(A)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{X\subseteq A}{\FormulaRefAuto{x \in \powerset(A)\;\eqvdash\; x \subseteq A}{2}}
  \proofstep{}{A\subseteq A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq A\cup B}}
  \proofstep{2}{X\subseteq A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \subseteq B, B \subseteq C \vdash A \subseteq C}{3,4}}
  \proofstep{}{a\in A\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\in A\cup\{a\}}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{t_{J_{A,a}}(X)=X\cup\{a\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep X\in \powerset(A) \vdash t_{J_{A,a}}(X)\coloneqq X\cup\{a\}}{1,2}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{t_{J_{A,a}}(X)\subseteq A\cup\{a\}}{\rIE{7,\FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq C\dsep b\in C \vdash A\cup\{b\}\subseteq C}{5,6}}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{t_{J_{A,a}}(X)\in \powerset(A\cup\{a\})}{\FormulaRefAuto{x \in \powerset(A)\;\eqvdash\; x \subseteq A}{8}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Potenzmengen-Adjunktion als Funktion]{%
  a\notin A \vdash J_{A,a}\colon \powerset(A)\to \powerset(A\cup\{a\})
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{t_{J_{A,a}}\dsep J_{A,a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\forall X\in \powerset(A)\,t_{J_{A,a}}(X)\in \powerset(A\cup\{a\})}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \dsep X\in \powerset(A) \vdash t_{J_{A,a}}(X)\in \powerset(A\cup\{a\})}{1}}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists! J\colon \powerset(A)\to \powerset(A\cup\{a\})\,\forall X\in \powerset(A)\,J(X)=t_{J_{A,a}}(X)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A\vdash t(x)\coloneqq y\dsep x\in A\vdash t(x)\in B\exists! F\colon A\to B\,\forall x\in A\,F(x)=t(x)}{2}}
  \proofstep{1}{J_{A,a}\colon \powerset(A)\to \powerset(A\cup\{a\})}{}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Injektivität von \(J_{A,a}\)]{%
  a\notin A\dsep X\in \powerset(A)\dsep Y\in \powerset(A)\dsep J_{A,a}(X)=J_{A,a}(Y)\vdash X=Y
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep X\dsep Y\dsep z}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{J_{A,a}}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{a\notin A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{X\in \powerset(A)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{Y\in \powerset(A)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{J_{A,a}(X)=J_{A,a}(Y)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2}{J_{A,a}(X)=X\cup\{a\}}{}
  \proofstep{1,3}{J_{A,a}(Y)=Y\cup\{a\}}{}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{X\cup\{a\}=Y\cup\{a\}}{\rIE{5,\rIE{4,\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{6}}}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{X=Y}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A\dsep X\subseteq A\dsep Y\subseteq A\dsep X\cup\{a\}=Y\cup\{a\}\vdash X=Y}{1,\FormulaRefAuto{x \in \powerset(A)\;\eqvdash\; x \subseteq A}{2},\FormulaRefAuto{x \in \powerset(A)\;\eqvdash\; x \subseteq A}{3},7}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Potenzmenge einer Adjunktion]{%
  a\notin A \vdash \Finite(\powerset(A\cup\{a\})) \leftrightarrow \Finite(\powerset(A)\cup J_{A,a}[\powerset(A)])
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep a\dsep X}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{J_{A,a}}
}

\FormulaThmDelta[Potenzmengen natürlicher Zahlen sind endlich]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Finite(\powerset(n))
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n\dsep u}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionensymbol}{J_{u,u}}
}
\begin{tabproofsplitwide}
  \proofpartwideind[Induktionsanfang]{\Finite(\powerset(\varnothing))}
    \proofstepwidestar{}{\powerset(\varnothing)=\{\varnothing\}}{\FormulaRefAuto{\powerset(\varnothing)=\{\varnothing\}}}
    \proofstepwidestar{}{\Finite(\{\varnothing\})}{\FormulaRefAuto{a\notin\varnothing \dsep \Finite(\varnothing) \vdash \Finite(\varnothing\cup\{a\})}{\FormulaRefAuto{x\notin\varnothing},\FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(\varnothing)}}}
    \proofstepwidestar{}{\Finite(\powerset(\varnothing))}{\rIE{1,2}}
  \closeproofpartwideind

  \proofpartwideind[Induktionsschritt]{%
    u\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \Finite(\powerset(u)) \vdash \Finite(\powerset(\Succ(u)))}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{u\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[2]{\Finite(\powerset(u))}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{u\notin u}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\notin n}{1}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\Finite(J_{u,u}[\powerset(u)])}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{C\subseteq A\dsep F\colon A\to B\dsep \Finite(C) \vdash \Finite(F[C])}{\FormulaRefAuto{\powerset(u)\subseteq\powerset(u)},\FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \vdash J_{A,a}\colon \powerset(A)\to \powerset(A\cup\{a\})}{3},2}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\Finite(\powerset(u)\cup J_{u,u}[\powerset(u)])}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{A\cap B=\varnothing \dsep \Finite(A)\dsep \Finite(B) \vdash \Finite(A\cup B)}{\FormulaRefAuto{\powerset(u)\cap J_{u,u}[\powerset(u)]=\varnothing}{3},2,4}}

    \proofstepwidestar[1,2]{\Finite(\powerset(\Succ(u)))}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{a\notin A \vdash \Finite(\powerset(A\cup\{a\})) \leftrightarrow \Finite(\powerset(A)\cup J_{A,a}[\powerset(A)])}{3,5}}
  \closeproofpartwideind

  \proofpartwide{Schluss}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
    \proofstepwidestar[1]{\Finite(\powerset(n))}{%
      \makecell[l]{%
        \FormulaRefAuto{P(\varnothing)\dsep \forall u\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(P(u)\rightarrow P(\Succ(u))\bigr)\vdash \forall u\in\mathbb{N}\,P(u)}(%
        \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(\powerset(\varnothing))},%
        \\ \quad \FormulaRefAuto{u\in\mathbb{N}\dsep \Finite(\powerset(u)) \vdash \Finite(\powerset(\Succ(u)))}%
        \\ \quad ,1)%
      }}
  \closeproofpartwide
\end{tabproofsplitwide}

\FormulaThmDelta[Potenzmengen gleichmächtiger Mengen sind gleichmächtig]{%
  A \EqCard B \vdash \powerset(A)\EqCard \powerset(B)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep B\dsep X\dsep Y}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{A\EqCard B}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists F\colon A\bij B}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{1}}
  \proofstep{3}{F\colon A\bij B}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\powerset(A)\EqCard \powerset(B)}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash \powerset(A)\EqCard \powerset(B)}{3}}
  \proofstep{1}{\powerset(A)\EqCard \powerset(B)}{\rEE{2,3,4}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta[Potenzmengen endlicher Mengen sind endlich]{%
  \Finite(A)\vdash \Finite(\powerset(A))
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{A\dsep n}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(A)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n\EqCard A\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{1}}

  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land n\EqCard A}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{n\EqCard A}{\rAEb{3}}
  \proofstep{4}{\Finite(\powerset(n))}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \Finite(\powerset(n))}{4}}
  \proofstep{5}{\powerset(n)\EqCard \powerset(A)}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \vdash \powerset(A)\EqCard \powerset(B)}{5}}
  \proofstep{3}{\Finite(\powerset(A))}{\FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\dsep M \EqCard N \vdash \Finite(N)}{6,7}}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(\powerset(A))}{\rEE{2,3,8}}
\end{tabproof}

\section{Wohldefiniertheit der Kardinalität}

\subsection{Eindeutigkeit der endlichen Kardinalität}

\FormulaThmDelta[Selbstinjektionen natürlicher Zahlen sind bijektiv]{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\inj n \vdash F\colon n\bij n
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{n}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon n\inj n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{n \EqCard n}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard A}}
  \proofstep{1}{\neg\exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\inj n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n \EqCard M\vdash \neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{1,3}}
  \proofstep{1}{\neg\exists G\colon n\sur \mathbb{N}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M \vdash \neg\exists F\colon M\sur \mathbb{N}}{4}}
  \proofstep{1}{\forall G\colon n\inj n\,\bigl(G\colon n\bij n\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\neg\exists F\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}\vdash \forall F\colon M\inj M\,\bigl(F\colon M\bij M\bigr)}{5}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{F\colon n\bij n}{\rUE{6}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Keine größere natürliche Zahl ist gleichmächtig]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in n \vdash {}\\
    &\neg(m \EqCard n)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in n \vdash \neg(m \EqCard n)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{m\dsep n\dsep x}
  \DeltaRow{Funktionen}{F\dsep G}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{m\in n}{\rA}

  \proofstep{4}{m \EqCard n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{n \EqCard m}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \vdash B \EqCard A}{4}}
  \proofstep{4}{\exists F\colon n\bij m}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{5}}

  \proofstep{7}{F\colon n\bij m}{\rA}
  \proofstep{7}{F\colon n\to m}{\FormulaRefAuto{Bijektive Funktion}{7}}
  \proofstep{7}{F\colon n\inj m}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F\colon A\inj B}{7}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{m\subset n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in n \vdash m\subset n}{1,2,3}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{m\subseteq n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subset B\vdash A\subseteq B}{10}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\iota_{m,n}\colon m\inj n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B\vdash \iota_{A,B}\colon A\inj B}{11}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,7}{\iota_{m,n}\circ F\colon n\inj n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B \dsep G\colon B\inj C\vdash G\circ F\colon A\inj C}{9,12}}

  \proofstep{2,13}{\iota_{m,n}\circ F\colon n\bij n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep F\colon n\inj n \vdash F\colon n\bij n}{2,13}}
  \proofstep{2,13}{\iota_{m,n}\circ F\colon n\sur n}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F\colon A\sur B}{14}}

  \proofstep{2,3,13}{\exists x\in n\,(\iota_{m,n}\circ F)(x)=m}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\sur B \dsep y\in B \vdash \exists x\in A\,F(x)=y}{15,3}}

  \proofstep{17}{x\in n\land (\iota_{m,n}\circ F)(x)=m}{\rA}
  \proofstep{17}{x\in n}{\rAEa{17}}
  \proofstep{17}{(\iota_{m,n}\circ F)(x)=m}{\rAEb{17}}

  \proofstep{7,18}{F(x)\in m}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{8,18}}
  \proofstep{18}{(\iota_{m,n}\circ F)(x)=\iota_{m,n}(F(x))}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{x\in A \vdash (F\circ G)(x)=F(G(x))}{18}}
  \proofstep{11,20}{\iota_{m,n}(F(x))=F(x)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A\subseteq B \dsep x\in A \vdash \iota_{A,B}(x)=x}{11,20}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,7,17}{(\iota_{m,n}\circ F)(x)=F(x)}{\rIE{21,22}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,7,17}{F(x)=m}{\rIE{\FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{23},19}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,7,17}{m\in m}{\rIE{24,20}}
  \proofstep{1}{m\notin m}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash n\notin n}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,7,17}{\bot}{\rBI{25,26}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3,7}{\bot}{\rEE{16,17,27}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\neg(m \EqCard n)}{\rCI{4,28}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Eindeutigkeit der endlichen Kardinalität]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep{}\\
    &n \EqCard M\dsep m \EqCard M \vdash n=m
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n \EqCard M\dsep m \EqCard M \vdash n=m
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{m\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n \EqCard M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{4}{m \EqCard M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{4}{M \EqCard m}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \vdash B \EqCard A}{4}}
  \proofstep{3,4}{n \EqCard m}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \dsep B \EqCard C \vdash A \EqCard C}{3,5}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{n\in m\lor m\in n\lor n=m}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash m\in n\lor n\in m\lor m=n}{2,1}}

  \proofstep{8}{n\in m}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1,2,8}{\neg(n \EqCard m)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in n \vdash \neg(m \EqCard n)}{1,2,8}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4,8}{n=m}{\FormulaRefAuto{P,\,\neg P \vdash Q}{6,9}}

  \proofstep{11}{m\in n}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{m \EqCard n}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \vdash B \EqCard A}{6}}
  \proofstep{2,1,11}{\neg(m \EqCard n)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in n \vdash \neg(m \EqCard n)}{2,1,11}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3,4,11}{n=m}{\FormulaRefAuto{P,\,\neg P \vdash Q}{12,13}}

  \proofstep{15}{n=m}{\rA}
  \proofstep{15}{n=m}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2,3,4}{n=m}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{P_1\lor P_2\lor P_3\dsep [P_1]\vdots R\dsep [P_2]\vdots R\dsep [P_3]\vdots R\vdash R}{7,8,10,11,14,15,16}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Definition der Kardinalität}

\FormulaThmDelta[Wohldefiniertheit der Kardinalität]{%
  \Finite(M)\vdash \exists! n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M\bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep m}
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\Finite(M)}{\rA}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M\bigr)}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{\Finite(M)\coloneqq \exists n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(n \EqCard M\bigr)}{1}}

  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{3}}
  \proofstep{3}{n \EqCard M}{\rAEb{3}}

  \proofstep{6}{m\in\mathbb{N}\land m \EqCard M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{6}{m\in\mathbb{N}}{\rAEa{6}}
  \proofstep{6}{m \EqCard M}{\rAEb{6}}

  \proofstep{3,6}{n=m}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep m\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n \EqCard M\dsep m \EqCard M \vdash n=m}{4,7,5,8}}

  \proofstep{1}{\exists! n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M\bigr)}{\UEI{2,3,6,9}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaDefDelta[Funktionsvorschrift der Kardinalität]{%
  \Finite(M)\vdash \tCard(M) \coloneqq \iota n\,\bigl(n\in\mathbb{N}\land n \EqCard M\bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep n}
  \DeltaRow{Termsymbol}{\tCard}
}

\section{Äquivalente Formulierungen der Endlichkeit}

\subsection[Ausschluss von Injektionen N -> M]{%
  Ausschluss von Injektionen \(\mathbb{N}\to M\)}

\FormulaThmDelta{%
    n\in\mathbb{N}\dsep n \EqCard M\vdash \neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M %
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{n\dsep M}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{n \EqCard M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{3}{\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{\exists G\colon n\bij M}{\FormulaRefAuto{A \EqCard B \coloneqq \exists F\colon A\bij B}{2}}

  \proofstep{5}{G\colon n\bij M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{5}{G^{-1}\colon M\bij n}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F^{-1}\colon B\bij A}{5}}
  \proofstep{5}{G^{-1}\colon M\inj n}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F\colon A\inj B}{6}}

  \proofstep{8}{F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{5,8}{G^{-1}\circ F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj n}{\FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B \dsep G\colon B\inj C\vdash G\circ F\colon A\inj C}{8,7}}

  \proofstep{5,8}{\exists H\colon \mathbb{N}\inj n}{\rEI{9}}
  \proofstep{1}{\neg\exists H\colon \mathbb{N}\inj n}{\FormulaRefAuto{n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj n}{1}}
  \proofstep{1,5,8}{\bot}{\rBI{10,11}}

  \proofstep{1,3,5}{\bot}{\rEE{3,8,12}}
  \proofstep{1,2,3}{\bot}{\rEE{4,5,13}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rCI{3,14}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection[Injektionen N -> M und Surjektionen M -> N]{%
  Injektionen \(\mathbb{N}\to M\) und Surjektionen \(M\to \mathbb{N}\)}
\FormulaThmDelta{%
  \exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M\vdash
  \exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{G\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{G\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{}{\varnothing\in\mathbb{N}}{\FormulaRefAuto{\varnothing \in \mathbb{N}}}

  \proofstep{2}{\Gsurjfrominj{G}{\varnothing}\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a_0\in A \vdash \Gsurjfrominj{F}{a_0}\colon B\sur A}{3}}

  \proofstep{2}{\exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{\rEI{4}}

  \proofstep{1}{\exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{\rEE{1,2,5}}
\end{tabproof}



\FormulaThmDelta{%
  \neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M
  \vdash
  \neg\exists F\colon M\sur \mathbb{N}%
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{F\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{\exists F\colon M\sur \mathbb{N}}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{F\colon M\sur \mathbb{N}}{\rA}

  \proofstep{3}{\exists H\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\sur B\vdash \exists H\colon B\inj A}{3}}

  \proofstep{1,3}{\bot}{\rBI{1,4}}
  \proofstep{1,2}{\bot}{\rEE{2,3,5}}
  \proofstep{1}{\neg\exists F\colon M\sur \mathbb{N}}{\rCI{2,6}}
\end{tabproof}



\FormulaThmDeltaR{%
  \exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M
  \eqvdash
  \exists F\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}
}{%
  \exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M
  \eqvdash
  \exists F\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{F\dsep G\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproofsplit}
  \proofpart{\(\vdash\)}
    \proofstep{1}{\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rA}
    \proofstep{1}{\exists F\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{%
        \exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M\vdash
        \exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}
      }{1}}
  \closeproofpart

  \proofpart{\(\dashv\)}
    \proofstep{1}{\exists F\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

    \proofstep{2}{\neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rA}
    \proofstep{2}{\neg\exists F\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{%
      \FormulaRefAuto{%
        \neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M
        \vdash
        \neg\exists F\colon M\sur \mathbb{N}
      }{2}}

    \proofstep{1,2}{\bot}{\rBI{1,3}}
    \proofstep{1}{\neg\neg\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rCI{2,4}}
    \proofstep{1}{\exists F\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\FormulaRefAuto{rDN}{5}}
  \closeproofpart
\end{tabproofsplit}



\subsection{Dedekindsche Charakterisierung endlicher Mengen}

\subsubsection{Orbit einer injektiven Selbstabbildung}

\FormulaThmDeltaR[Kein echter Folgewert ist der Startwert]{%
  \begin{aligned}[t]
    &m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep{}\\
    &\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\vdash{}\\
    &\forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))\neq m_0
    \bigr)
  \end{aligned}
}{%
  m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep
  \forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\vdash
  \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))\neq m_0
  \bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep n\dsep x\dsep m_0}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{f}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{3}{\forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{f\colon M\to M}{\FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{2}}

  \proofstep{5}{n\in\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M \vdash \RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\to M}{1,4}}

  \proofstep{1,2,5}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n)\in M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\to B\dsep x\in A\vdash F(x)\in B}{6,5}}

  \proofstep{1,2,5}{%
    \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\to M\dsep n\in\mathbb{N}\vdash \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))}{1,4,5}}

  \proofstep{9}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))=m_0}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,2,5}{%
    f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))=\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b\vdash b=a}{8}}

  \proofstep{1,2,5,9}{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))=m_0}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{a=b,\, b=c \vdash a=c}{10,9}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3,5}{f(\RecFun{m_0}{f}(n))\neq m_0}{%
    \rRE{\rUE{3},7}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3,5,9}{\bot}{\rBI{11,12}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3,5}{\RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))\neq m_0}{\rCI{9,13}}

  \proofstep{1,2,3}{%
    \forall n\in\mathbb{N}\,\bigl(
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}(\Succ(n))\neq m_0
    \bigr)
  }{%
    \rUI{\rRI{5,14}}}
\end{tabproof}




\subsubsection{Dedekindsche Charakterisierung}

% =========================================================
% Hauptsatz:  ¬∃(M ↠ N)  ->  jede Selbstinjektion ist Bijektion
% =========================================================
\FormulaThmDelta{%
  \neg\exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}\vdash
  \forall F\colon M\inj M\,\bigl(F\colon M\bij M\bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep m_0\dsep x}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{F\dsep G\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\neg\exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{F\colon M\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{2}{F\colon M\to M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{Injektive Funktion}{2}}

  \proofstep{4}{\neg(F\colon M\sur M)}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2,4}{%
    \exists m_0\in M\,\forall x\in M\,\bigl(F(x)\neq m_0\bigr)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      F\colon M\to M\dsep \neg(F\colon M\sur M)\vdash
      \exists m_0\in M\,\forall x\in M\,\bigl(F(x)\neq m_0\bigr)
    }{3,4}}

  \proofstep{6}{m_0\in M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{7}{%
    \forall x\in M\,\bigl(F(x)\neq m_0\bigr)
  }{\rA}

  \proofstep{2,6,7}{%
    \RecFun{m_0}{F}\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      m_0\in M\dsep f\colon M\inj M\dsep
      \forall x\in M\,\bigl(f(x)\neq m_0\bigr)\vdash
      \RecFun{m_0}{f}\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M
    }{6,2,7}}

  \proofstep{2,6,7}{\exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M}{\rEI{8}}

  \proofstep{2,6,7}{\exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      \exists G\colon \mathbb{N}\inj M\vdash
      \exists H\colon M\sur\mathbb{N}
    }{9}}

  \proofstep{1,2,6,7}{\bot}{\rBI{1,10}}

  \proofstep{1,2,4}{\bot}{\rEE{5,6,7,11}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{F\colon M\sur M}{\rCI{4,12}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{F\colon M\bij M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B\dsep F\colon A\sur B \vdash F\colon A\bij B}{2,13}}

  \proofstep{1}{%
    \forall F\colon M\inj M\,\bigl(F\colon M\bij M\bigr)
  }{\rUI{\rRI{2,14}}}
\end{tabproof}

\FormulaThmDelta{%
  \forall F\colon M\inj M\,\bigl(F\colon M\bij M\bigr)\vdash
  \forall F\colon M\sur M\,\bigl(F\colon M\bij M\bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaDecl{Mengen}{M\dsep y}%
  \DeltaDecl{Funktionen}{F\dsep H}%
}
\begin{tabproof}
  \proofstep{1}{\forall F\colon M\inj M\,\bigl(F\colon M\bij M\bigr)}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{F\colon M\sur M}{\rA}

  \proofstep{2}{%
    \exists H\colon M\inj M\,\forall y\in M\,\bigl(F(H(y))=y\bigr)
  }{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
      F\colon A\sur B\vdash
      \exists H\colon B\inj A\,\forall y\in B\,\bigl(F(H(y))=y\bigr)
    }{2}}

  \proofstep{4}{H\colon M\inj M}{\rA}
  \proofstep{5}{\forall y\in M\,\bigl(F(H(y))=y\bigr)}{\rA}

  \proofstep{1,4}{H\colon M\bij M}{\rRE{\rUE{1},4}}
  \proofstep{1,4}{H\colon M\sur M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\bij B \vdash F\colon A\sur B}{6}}

  \proofstep{1,4,5}{F\colon M\inj M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{%
        G\colon A\sur B\dsep F\colon B\to A\dsep
          \forall y\in B\,\bigl(G(F(y))=y\bigr)\vdash
          F\colon B\inj A
    }{7,5}}

  \proofstep{1,2,4,5}{F\colon M\bij M}{%
    \FormulaRefAuto{F\colon A\inj B\dsep F\colon A\sur B \vdash F\colon A\bij B}{8,2}}

  \proofstep{1,2}{F\colon M\bij M}{\rEE{3,4,5,9}}

  \proofstep{1}{%
    \forall F\colon M\sur M\,\bigl(F\colon M\bij M\bigr)
  }{\rUI{\rRI{2,10}}}
\end{tabproof}

\subsection{Tarskische Charakterisierung endlicher Mengen}

\subsubsection{Axiom der Tarski-Endlichkeit}

\FormulaAxiomDelta[Tarskisches Maximalitätsaxiom]{%
  B\subseteq \powerset(M)\dsep B\neq\varnothing \vdash
  \exists x\in B\,\forall y\in B\,\bigl(x\subseteq y \rightarrow y=x\bigr)
}{%
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep B\dsep x\dsep y}
}

\subsubsection{Definition der Tarski-Endlichkeit}

\FormulaDefDeltaK[Begriff der Tarski-Endlichkeit]{%
  \TarskiFinite(M)
}{Tarski-endliche Menge}{
  \DeltaRow{Mengen}{M\dsep B\dsep x\dsep y}
  \DeltaRow{\textbf{Axiome}}{}
  \DeltaRow{\makecell[l]{Tarskisches\\Maximalitätsaxiom}}
  {%
    \begin{aligned}[t]
      &B\subseteq \powerset(M)\dsep B\neq\varnothing \vdash{}\\
      &\exists x\in B\,\forall y\in B\,\bigl(x\subseteq y \rightarrow y=x\bigr)
    \end{aligned}
  }
  [%
    \FormulaRefAuto{B\subseteq \powerset(M)\dsep B\neq\varnothing \vdash \exists x\in B\,\forall y\in B\,\bigl(x\subseteq y \rightarrow y=x\bigr)}%
  ]
  \DeltaRow{\textbf{Neue Symbole}}{}
  \DeltaPrem{Tarski-endliche Mengen}{ }
}
